Tom was biased.	Tom war voreingenommen.

Tom was caught.	Tom wurde erwischt.
Tom was clever.	Tom war clever.
Tom was clever.	Tom war klug.
Tom was crafty.	Tom war schlau.
Tom was cranky.	Tom war launisch.
Tom was crying.	Tom weinte.
Tom was crying.	Tom heulte.
Tom was crying.	Tom flennte.
